Gets an {\ttfamily O\-W\-L\-Literal}, which has the specified lexical value, and is typed with the specified datatype.


\begin{DoxyParams}{Parameters}
{\em lexical\-Value} & The lexical value. Cannot be null. \\
\hline
{\em datatype} & The datatype. Cannot be null. \\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}
\begin{DoxyReturn}{Returns}
An O\-W\-L\-Literal with the specified lexical value and specified datatype. If the datatype is {\ttfamily rdf\-:Plain\-Literal}, and the lexical value contains a language tag then the language tag will be parsed out of the lexical value. For example, \char`\"{}abc@en\char`\"{}$^\wedge$$^\wedge$rdf\-:Plain\-Literal would be parsed into a lexical value of \char`\"{}abc\char`\"{} and a language tag of \char`\"{}en\char`\"{}. 
\end{DoxyReturn}

\subsubsection[{get\-O\-W\-L\-Literal}]{\setlength{\rightskip}{0pt plus 5cm}{\bf O\-W\-L\-Literal} uk.\-ac.\-manchester.\-cs.\-owl.\-owlapi.\-O\-W\-L\-Data\-Factory\-Impl.\-get\-O\-W\-L\-Literal (
\begin{DoxyParamCaption}
\item[{String}]{literal, }
\item[{String}]{lang}
\end{DoxyParamCaption}
)}}\label{classuk_1_1ac_1_1manchester_1_1cs_1_1owl_1_1owlapi_1_1_o_w_l_data_factory_impl_a8707f60c1be458306718c2d455c29860}
Gets an O\-W\-L\-Literal with a language tag. The datatype of this literal will have an I\-R\-I of rdf\-:Plain\-Literal ( \hyperlink{enumorg_1_1semanticweb_1_1owlapi_1_1vocab_1_1_o_w_l_r_d_f_vocabulary_a01c2f8d91e14f1b3ce7b2470bf641f50}{org.\-semanticweb.\-owlapi.\-vocab.\-O\-W\-L\-R\-D\-F\-Vocabulary\#\-R\-D\-F\-\_\-\-P\-L\-A\-I\-N\-\_\-\-L\-I\-T\-E\-R\-A\-L}).


\begin{DoxyParams}{Parameters}
{\em literal} & The string literal. Cannot be null. \\
\hline
{\em lang} & The language tag. The empty string may be specified to indicate an empty language tag. Leading and trailing white space will be removed from the tag and the tag will be normalised to L\-O\-W\-E\-R C\-A\-S\-E. If {\ttfamily lang} is {\ttfamily null} then {\ttfamily lang} will be converted to the empty string (for backwards compatibility). If not empty, the tag is formed according to \href{http://www.rfc-editor.org/rfc/bcp/bcp47.txt}{\tt B\-C\-P47} but the O\-W\-L A\-P\-I will not check that the tag conforms to this specification -\/ it is up to the caller to ensure this. \\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}
\begin{DoxyReturn}{Returns}
The O\-W\-L\-Literal that represents the string literal with a (possibly empty) language tag. 
\end{DoxyReturn}

\begin{DoxyParams}{Parameters}
{\em literal} & The string literal. Cannot be null. \\
\hline
{\em lang} & The language tag. The tag is formed according to \href{http://www.rfc-editor.org/rfc/bcp/bcp47.txt}{\tt B\-C\-P47} but the O\-W\-L A\-P\-I will not check that the tag conforms to this specification -\/ it is up to the caller to ensure this. For backwards compatibility, if the value of lang is {\ttfamily null} then this is equivalent to calling the \hyperlink{classuk_1_1ac_1_1manchester_1_1cs_1_1owl_1_1owlapi_1_1_o_w_l_data_factory_impl_af72d29fa0f65a9e4469358333bf2fb0b}{get\-O\-W\-L\-String\-Literal(\-String literal)} method. \\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}

The O\-W\-L\-String\-Literal that represents the string literal with a language tag. 
\end{DoxyReturn}

S\-W\-R\-L provides a core set of builtins, which are described in the O\-W\-L A\-P\-I by the \hyperlink{enumorg_1_1semanticweb_1_1owlapi_1_1vocab_1_1_s_w_r_l_built_ins_vocabulary}{org.\-semanticweb.\-owlapi.\-vocab.\-S\-W\-R\-L\-Built\-Ins\-Vocabulary}.


\begin{DoxyParams}{Parameters}

\hline

\hline
\end{DoxyParams}

\begin{DoxyExceptions}{Exceptions}
{\em Illegal\-Argument\-Exception} & if the list of arguments is empty \\
\hline
\end{DoxyExceptions}
\begin{DoxyReturn}{Returns}
A S\-W\-R\-L\-Built\-In\-Atom whose predicate is identified by the specified built\-In\-I\-R\-I and that has the specified arguments 
\end{DoxyReturn}
